 Beware of playing robot toys and video games with a headset
 havers in logon ke dimag main chal rahe vichaaron kii nigaraanee karke unke pin or password kaa pataa laga sakate hai
 According to scientists, brainwave sensing headsets need more protection
 vaigyanikon main bhartiya mul kaa ek vyakti bhi shaamil he
 With electrosyphalograph (EEG) headsets, users control robotic toys and video games with their brains
 america main birmingham main albama vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakartaaon ne yah pataa lagaaya ki video game khel rahe ek vyakti ne agar game ko bich main hi roak diya or vah iiji hedset pahane hue bank khate main log in karata he to us par hekking karne vaale kisi software dwaara password yaa anya samvedansheel aankade chori hone kaa khatra paidaa ho jaataa he
 The team of scientists used an EEG headset available online to consumers and a clinical grade headset used for scientific research to show how easily hacking software can detect what is going on in the user's brain
 Can
 tippaniyan While typing there are activities in the nerves of the user's hands, eyes and brain
 ye sabhi gatividhiyaan iiji hedsets main record ho jaati he
 Hacking software has access to these records
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) electrocyphelograph (iiji) hedsets se yugers apane dimag se robotic khilaunon or video game ko niyantrit karte hai

 jabaki 14,962 green card bahan-bhai kii category main jari kiye gaye
 The number of green card holders is declining, according to a report released by the Department of Homeland Security (DHS) on 2 October, the number of green card holders has decreased in the last two years

 sansad ne do aise vidheyak paarit kiye hai jo desh main aalaa adaalat ke jajon kii niyukti ke tareeke ko moolbhoot rup se badal denge

 sarkaar shaayad jajon kii niyukt main collegium system par chaaron taraf se ho rahe hamale kaa phayda uthaanaa chaahati thi

 1993 se aalaa adaalat ke jajon kii niyukt collegium system ke tahat hoti rahi he
 The system consists of senior judges and they appoint judges
 lekin is vyavastha main khulaapan na hone or javabdehi tay na hone kii baat kahkar isaki aalochana hoti thi
 These Bills have been proposed to replace the Collegium system with the National Judicial Appointments Commission (NJAC)
 engeesi main chah sadsy hongeh pradhan nyaayadhish (sijei), ‚Äòsupreme court ke do varisht jaj‚Äô, do ‚Äòpratishthit vyakdwait‚Äô or kanoon mantri
 It has the minister as the sole political member
 chunki ‚Äòpratishthit vyakddhityon‚Äô kaa chayan ek samiti karegi, jisamen pradhan nyaayadhish or ek-duusare ke virdohi pradhanmantri va vipaksh ke netaa honge, isliye ‚Äòpratishthit vyakdwait‚Äô sambhavat: nirdaleey or nishpaksh honge
 The new NJAC will have three judicial members and three non-judicial members
 nyaayik or gaiyr-nyaayik sadasyon ke bich is samaan santulan par kisi ko aapatti nahin ho sakati
 Until now, the process of judicial appointments in the country was described as one-sided, in which either the executive had complete 'supremacy' over the judiciary or the judiciary over the executive
 is prakaar 1981 main ‚Äòfasrt jajej cese‚Äô main supreme court ne faisla diya ki karypalika ko nyaayik niyuktiyon kii prakriya main sarvocchata hasil hogi, jabaki 1993 main ‚Äòsecond jajej cese‚Äô main nyaaypalika ko pramukhataa hasil ho gai thi
 Now both of these will get equal rights in appointment of judges from these new Bills
 baharhaal, engeesi ke maujuuda swaroop main kuch gambhir khamiyaan hai
 The first, which is perhaps the most important, is that the process of voting in NJAC can be dangerously changed at any time by the government
 sansad ne do nae kanoon paarit kiye hai‚Äîsamvidhan (99waan sanshodhan) kanoon, 2014 (jise prabhaav main aane ke liye ab bhi rajyon kii aadhi vidhansabhaon ke anumodan kii jarurat he) or neshnal juditial epointments kamishan kanoon, 2014
 At this time, the voting process only comes in other laws
 yah kahata he ki engeesi 5-1 ke maha-bahumat ke aadhaar par jajon kii niyuktiyaan karegaa‚Äîengeesi ke kinhin bhi do sadasyon ko jajon kii niyukti par vito lagane kaa adhikaar hoga
 This is satisfactory, because in this the appointments of judges can be made non-political without the consent of the sole political member ie Law Minister
 lekin voting kii is vyavastha ko sanvaidhanik sanshodhan main nirdhaarit nahin kiya gaya he, balki saadhaaran kanoon main nirdhaarit kiya he, isliye jarurat ke samay sansad dwaara ise kisi bhi samay badla ja saktaa he
 It is not easy to amend the provisions of the Constitution in the matter of judicial appointments in the country
 aisa ke liye sansad main do-tihaai bahumat kii jarurat hoti he or rajyon kii vidhansabhaon se anumodan praapt karnaa hota he
 In contrast, ordinary laws can be passed by a simple majority in Parliament
 is prakaar nyaayik niyukti ayog sambandhi kanoon ko sansad saadhaaran bahumat ke jariye kabhi bhi badla ja saktaa he
 Second, NJAC is too much centralized
 collegium system main sthaneey hycourt ke collejiyamon ko hycourt ke jajon kii niyuktiyon main pramukh bhoomika hasil hoti he
 In contrast, the NJAC is a purely central institution with no place for local representation
 apane rajyon kii jamini hakikaton se waakif hycourt ke mukhya nyaayadhishon ko engeesi main koi bhoomika hasil nahin he
 Further, why should the Union Minister have the right to decide who will be the judge in the Madras High Court
 nae kanoon main engeesi ko hycourt ke mukhya nyaayadhishon or rajya sarkaron kii siforeeshon par sirf vichaar karne kii jarurat he, lekin un siforeeshon ko puri tarah andekha kiya ja saktaa he
 There is no restriction on this
 teesri, haalanki nyaayik niyuktiyon kii pranali badal gai he, lekin logon ko ashanka he ki nyaayik niyuktiyon main gaharaai se paithe paaramparik taur-tareeke main shaayad koi badlaav aayega
 Presently, there are unwritten rules that a person below 55 years of age cannot be appointed a judge of the Supreme Court and only 'senior' judges (mostly Chief Justice of the High Court) can become judges of the Supreme Court
 jabaki iske liye yogyata ko aadhaar maananaa chahie, na ki umr or varishthata ko
 There is no system to change this trend in NJAC
 agar is tarah kii vyavastha daali jaati to apekshaakrit urjavan, yogya or yuva jajon ko bhi supreme court main aane kaa mauka mil paata
 There are some other problems with these bills
 99waan samvidhan sanshodhan is baat ko spasht nahin karata he ki raashtrapati kya engeesi kii siforeeshon ko maanane ke liye baadhya hai
 In addition, NJAC has a majority of non-judicial members in the selection of the Chief Justice
 sankshep main kahen to collegium vyavastha main haalanki kuch sudhaar kii jarurat thi, lekin jaldbaaji main taiyaar kiye gaye maujuuda vidheyakon main kai gambhir galtiyaan hai, jin par gaharaai se gaur karne kii jarurat he
